          <h2 class="postTitle">
           <a class="exit_menu" href="https://mobile.its.umich.edu/michigan/dining#/">
           </a>
           <span class="titleText">
            Bursley
           </span>
           <a class="home_button" href="https://mobile.its.umich.edu/michigan/home">
           </a>
          </h2>
          <ul class="location-details">
